 hoicourt or supreme court ke jajon kii niyukti ke liye banaae gaye neshnal jeudicial appointment kamishan (NJAC) act ke khilaaf daakhil yachika par sunwaayee ke dauraan centre ne act kaa bachaav kiya
 The Center, in its reply, clarified the role of the President in the appointment of judges, saying that in these cases the President takes part only formally
 supreme court ne is dauraan kaha kinyaaypalika kii swatantraaor shakti santulan kii baat sarkaar bhi maanati he, isse aage kya kahana he
 On this, the Center said that the talk of independence of the judiciary starts when judges are appointed, not before that
 engeesi main bhi nyaayik swatantraaa kaayam rahegi
 The system of appointing judges through the NJAC instead of the collegium system will be more transparent and accountable
 court ko bataaya gaya ki sansad ke saath 20 rajyon kii vidhansabhaon ne bhi NJAC kaa paksh liya he
 Attorney General Mukul Rohatgi argued that NJAC is limiting executive rights
 sunwaayee ke dauraan supreme court ne centre se yah bataane ko kaha ki anuchhed-124 ke tahat raashtrapati jab salaah se jajon kii niyukti karte hai, to kya yah raashtrapati kaa visheshadhikaar ke daayre main he yaa sarkaar ke madhyam se is adhikaar kaa istemaal hota he
 To this, the Attorney General said that when the President appoints judges, it is ceremonial and formal
 darasal unhen pradhanmantri kii aguai main mantriparishad salaah detii he
 The Attorney General said that the appointment of the judges was in fact an executive function and the President was to issue directions for role appointment

 itnaa hi nahin, vah bal vivaah rokane ke liye kaam kar rahi he or uski kahaniyaan saajha karne ke liye use pichley saal sanyukt raashtra mahasabha main aamantrit bhi kiya gaya tha
 Leaving her daughters-in-law and husband-in-law, Santana takes a three-kilometer walk from Kushmandi village in South Dinajpur district to Manikore High School every morning
 yah silsilaa chaar saal ke antaraal ke baad pichley saptaah shuru hua
 Santana Murmu's elder daughter Vasundhara is three years old and attends Anganwadi Play School
 padhai ko lekar utsahit santna ne news agency bhashaa ko bataaya, 'main bahut romanchit hum
 i am the oldest in the class and everybody respects me a lot
 main teacher banakar apane sapane puure karnaa chaahati hum
 In this new journey of life, Santana's husband Gobind Hemram and members of the non-governmental organization 'child in Need Institute' (CINI) are constantly supporting her
 gobind mazdooree karte hai or paanchavi kaksha main hi padhai chhod chuke hai
 He says, 'I am proud of him and also realize that if we had not been married so soon, his life would have been better
 shiksha or swasthya bahut jaruri hai, isliye main uskaa saath de rahaa hum
 'before the girl became a bride, Santana dreamed of becoming a teacher
 unke pita ne apane bete ko to padhaayaa, lekin bitiyaa kii baari ai to unka rukh badal gaya
 Santana said, 'suddenly one day i was told that i was going to get married
 tab main apane vivaah ko rokane yaa padhai jari rakhane ke liye kuch bhi nahin kar saki
 But now i convinced my husband
 ' ab santna nahin chaahatin ki or koi balika vadhu bane
 Therefore, he is active in stopping child marriage
 santna ne saamaajik dabaav banaakar adivasee santhali samudaay kii teen ladakiyon kaa bal vivaah rukvaa diya
 In this community, after menstruation, girls are considered to be married
 tippaniyan Meanwhile, Santhana became associated with CINI
 unke kaam ne logon kaa dhyaan khinchaa or pichley saal sanyukt raashtra mahasabha main unhen aamantrit kiya gaya
 Santana's story about 'preventing maternal deaths by preventing child marriage' was heard in the United Nations General Assembly
 america main logon ne santna kii padhai ke bare main poocha to yah sawaal unhen gaharaai tak chubh gaya
 'I felt bad for stating that i had only studied till eighth grade
 tab maine unase kaha ki apane gaanv jane ke baad main phir se padhai karuungi
 And i did it too
 ' It was not easy to enroll in school
 siaienai ke sujay roy ne kaha 'shuru main to headmaster ne use manaa hi kar diya, lekin block dawalpment officer ke hastkshep se yah sambhav ho gaya
 'some people even got tearful for Santana studying in class ninth, but she did not care
 roy ne kaha, 'kuch log usase bahut naaraaz bhi hue kyonki usne bal vivaah kii barason puraani parampara ko chunauti di
 But she did not get discouraged

 ' Enthused about the study Santana told the news agency Bhasha, 'I am very thrilled
 kaksha main sabase zyada umr kii hum or sab log mujhe bahut sammaan dete hai
 i want to fulfill my dreams by becoming a teacher
 ' jindagi ke is nae safar main santna ke pati gobind hemaram or gaiyr-sarkari sanghathan 'child in nid institute' (siaienai) ke sadsy lagaataar unka saath de rahe hai
 Gobind works as a laborer and has dropped out of class five
 unka kahana he, 'mujhe us par garv he or yah ehsaas bhi he ki agar hamaari shaadi itani jald nahin hui hoti to uskaa jivan behatar hota
 Education and health are very important, so i am supporting him
 ' balika vadhu banane se pehle santna teacher banane kaa sapana dekhati thim
 His father taught his son, but his attitude changed when the daughter came
 santna ne bataaya, 'achaanak ek din mujhe kaha gaya ki meraa vivaah hone ja rahaa he
 Then i could not do anything to stop my marriage or to continue my studies
 lekin ab maine apane pati ko manaa liya
 'now the child does not want any other girl to be a bride
 isliye, vah bal vivaah rokane ke liye sakriy hai
 Santana stopped the child marriage of three girls of the tribal Santhali community by creating social pressure
 is samudaay main masik dharm hone ke baad ladakiyon ko vivaah yogya maan liya jaataa he
 The comments isi dauraan santna siaienai se judin
 His work caught the attention of the people and he was invited to the United Nations General Assembly last year
 'bal vivaah par roak se matra mrityu rokane' ke bare main santna kii kahani sanyukt raashtra mahasabha main suni gai
 When people asked about Santana's studies in America, this question deeply shocked them
 'mujhe yah bataate hue buree lagi ki main sirf aathvin kaksha tak hi padhi hum
 Then i told them that after going to my village, i will study again
 or maine yah kiya bhi
 ' skool main daakhila lenaa aasaan nahin tha
 Sujay Roy of CINI said, 'initially the headmaster refused it, but it became possible with the intervention of the Block Development Officer
 ' nauveen kaksha main pard rahi santna ke liye kuch logon kii tyoriyaan bhi tanin, lekin usne parvaah nahin kii
 Roy said, 'some people were also very angry with him because he challenged the age-old tradition of child marriage
 lekin vah hatotsahit nahin hui
 ' gobind mazdooree karte hai or paanchavi kaksha main hi padhai chhod chuke hai
